**Purpose:** This table lists firmware links found in the dataentries and their status [OK|notfound].

**Task:**
  - Find broken links by searching for //notfound//.
  - If you know the correct/latest fw download link, click the dataentry link for editing.
  - Correct the //Firmware LEDE install/upgrade url// in the dataentry
  - Check if //LEDE supported current release// matches the release in the fw download link and correct it if needed.
  - You are done when there are no more broken links, i.e. all fw links in the dataentries are working.
